 agar aap dhumrapaan karte hai, to ye khabar padhane ke baad aap is aadat ko or zyada din paalna nahin chahenge
 Smoking affects not only health, but also functioning and income
 dhumrapaan karne vaale vyakti kii aamadani dhumrapaan na karne vaale vyakti se kaaphi kam hoti he
 a new research revealed this
 america kii stenford uniwarsity ke sahaayak professor or is shodh ke netritvkarta judith prochaska ne ek bayaan main kaha, "dhumrapaan se hone vaali swasthya haniyaan sadiyon se saamne aati rahi hai, lekin is shodh ke nishkarsho ne dhumrapaan se hone vaali vittiya haani kaa khulaasa kiya he
 " is nae shodh main judith or unke dal ne 131 beroggaar dhumrapaan pratibhaagiyon or 120 berozegaar dhumrapaan na karne vaale pratibhaagiyon kaa ek saal tak adhyayan kiya
 During this period, the participants were assessed in the first, sixth and then 12th months of the study
 judith ne bataaya ki shodh main dhumrapaan karne or na karne vaale pratibhaagiyon ke bich kai maamalon main antar paae gaye
 They reported that smoking participants, for example, lagged behind non-smoking participants in terms of age, education, and health, suggesting that smoking affects job-seeking ability
 shodh ke anusaar, dhumrapaan karne vaale pratibhaagiyon kii phir se rojgaar praapt karne kii dar dhumrapaan na karne vaale pratibhaagiyon se 24 pratishat kam rahi
 Judith said, we have found from the findings that smokers have to refuse a lot of difficulty in getting a job 
 tippaniyan The research is published in the American journal 'JAMA'

 baharhaal is ghatana ne meghalaya main chal rahe pratibandhit 'rat hole' khadaanon ko ek baar phir charchaa main laa diya he
 What is Rat Hole Mining? Most of the minerals in India are nationalized and their mining is possible only after government permission
 lekin purvottar ke adhikansh janajaatiy kshetron main aisi sthiti nahin he
 According to the 6th schedule of the constitution, land and minerals found in it are owned by the communities at the individual level
 yahi vajah he ki is sanvaidhanik adhikaar kii aad main nijee hitdharak avaidh khadaanon kaa sanchaalan karte hai
 On the other hand, coal mining in the northeast is not possible like other places in the country because its layer is much thinner than 2 meters
 iske saath hi takanic kaa istemaal apekshaakrit mahangaa he
 Hence mining in such mines is done through a long narrow tunnel, known as Rat hole mining
 rat hole khanan main bahut sankari surangon kii khudaai kii jaati he, jo aamtaur par keval 3-4 feet oonchi hoti hai jisamen pravesh kar majdoor (aksar bachche bhi) koyale kii nikasi karte hai
 The workers who go to these tunnels have digging tools and flashlight and have to come down through a ladder
 chunki meghalaya kaa yah kshetra desh main sarvaadhik varsha vaala kshetra he lihaaja in surangon main philson, achaanak pani bharne se durghatnaayen saamne aati rahati hai
 Why Rat Hole Mining Is Banned? In 2014, the National Green Authority (NGT) banned such mines as unscientific and unsafe
 engiti ke paas daayar kii gai yachika main assam dimasa chaatr sangh or dima hasao jila samiti ne bataaya tha ki meghalaya main rat-hole khanan ne kopili nadi (yah meghalaya or assam se hokar bahati he) ko amleey bana diya
 The NGT, citing a report in its order, said that roads around the mining areas are used to accumulate coal piles which are a major source of pollution in air, water and soil
 iske alaava engiti ke anusaar, barsaat ke mausam main rat-hole khanan kii vajah kaaphi durghatnaayen saamne ain he
 In which many other persons including employees, laborers died due to waterlogging in the mining areas

 It is believed that most of this production was obtained by rat-hole mining
